SELECT [r].[Id], [t].[SampleName] AS [Sample], [u].[FullName] AS [Employee], [r].[Version], [r].[IsApproved] AS [Approved], [r].[Status], [r].[FileName]
FROM [Reports] AS [r]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[SampleName]
    FROM [Samples] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [r].[SampleId] = [t].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[UserId]
    FROM [Employees] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [r].[EmployeeId] = [t0].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [t0].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
WHERE [r].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
